beginSubroutine: s32'gio_MaterialParam'
  if: (VARIABLE), 16
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), (VARIABLE), 109, (STATIC), 5000
      storeValue: (VARIABLE), 53, (STATIC), 1
      endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), (VARIABLE), 109, (STATIC), 10000
        storeValue: (VARIABLE), 53, (STATIC), 2
        endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: (VARIABLE), 53, (STATIC), 3
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), (VARIABLE), 53, (VARIABLE), 54
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), (VARIABLE), 53, (STATIC), 1
        storeValue: (VARIABLE), 54, (STATIC), 1
        setCmnMaterialParam: 18, 0, 30
        setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 0, 30
        storeValue: (VARIABLE), 380, (STATIC), 0
        storeValue: (VARIABLE), 381, (STATIC), 0
        endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), (VARIABLE), 109, (STATIC), 10000
          storeValue: (VARIABLE), 54, (STATIC), 2
          setCmnMaterialParam: 18, 0, 30
          setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 1000, 30
          storeValue: (VARIABLE), 380, (STATIC), 5
          storeValue: (VARIABLE), 381, (STATIC), 5
          createObject: s32'gio_tension01', (PLAYER)
          characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_GIO_04'
          endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: (VARIABLE), 54, (STATIC), 3
          setCmnMaterialParam: 18, 1000, 30
          setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 1000, 30
          storeValue: (VARIABLE), 380, (STATIC), 10
          storeValue: (VARIABLE), 381, (STATIC), 10
          createObject: s32'gio_tension02', (PLAYER)
          characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_GIO_05'
          endElse: 
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: (VARIABLE), 53, (STATIC), 1
    setCmnMaterialParam: 18, 0, 30
    setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 0, 30
    endElse: 
  endSubroutine:
